 (func $main (param $0 i32) (param $1 i32) (result i32)
  (local $2 i32)
  (local $3 i32)
  (local $4 i32)
  (local $5 i32)
  (local $6 i32)
  (local $7 i32)
  (local $8 i32)
  (local $scratch i32)
  (local $scratch_10 i32)
  ;; code offset: 0x399
  (global.set $global$0
   ;; code offset: 0x397
   (local.tee $8
    ;; code offset: 0x396
    (i32.sub
     ;; code offset: 0x392
     (global.get $global$0)
     ;; code offset: 0x394
     (i32.const 32)
    )
   )
  )
  ;; code offset: 0x39b
  (block $block1
   ;; code offset: 0x39d
   (block $block
    ;; code offset: 0x3a4
    (if
     ;; code offset: 0x3a3
     (i32.ge_s
      ;; code offset: 0x39f
      (local.get $0)
      ;; code offset: 0x3a1
      (i32.const 2)
     )
     (then
      ;; code offset: 0x3b2
      (br_if $block
       ;; code offset: 0x3b1
       (i32.gt_s
        ;; code offset: 0x3ad
        (local.tee $3
         ;; code offset: 0x3ab
         (call $atoi
          ;; code offset: 0x3a8
          (i32.load offset=4
           ;; code offset: 0x3a6
           (local.get $1)
          )
         )
        )
        ;; code offset: 0x3af
        (i32.const 0)
       )
      )
     )
    )
    ;; code offset: 0x3ba
    (drop
     ;; code offset: 0x3b8
     (call $puts
      ;; code offset: 0x3b5
      (i32.const 1050)
     )
    )
    ;; code offset: 0x3bd
    (local.set $5
     ;; code offset: 0x3bb
     (i32.const 1)
    )
    ;; code offset: 0x3bf
